href="/docs/healthcare/transaction-enrollment">transaction enrollments</a> that are still in <code>DRAFT</code> status. <p>Calling this endpoint completely overwrites the previous request record. You <strong>must</strong> provide all the information for the enrollment in the request, not just the properties you want to update.</p><div class="flex items-end justify-between gap-2"><h2 data-component-part="field-required-pill">Required</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The contact information for the provider. This is where the payer will send communications about the enrollment, if needed.</p>
<ul>
<li>Either <code>organizationName</code> <em>or</em> <code>firstName</code> and <code>lastName</code> are required.</li>
<li>The name and address should match exactly what the payer has on file for the provider. Some payers reject enrollment requests with addresses that don&#x27;t match their records.</li>
<li>If you&#x27;re submitting enrollment requests on a provider&#x27;s behalf, you may want to set the phone number or email to your own contact details. Do this when you want the payer to contact you about the enrollment status instead of the provider directly.</li>
<li>This contact information doesn&#x27;t need to match existing contacts defined on the provider record. It also doesn&#x27;t modify or replace contacts on the provider record.</li>

- 10</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>This property is required for payers that require a Provider Transaction Access Number (PTAN).</p>
<p>The PTAN is a Medicare-issued number given to providers upon enrollment with Medicare. This number is usually six digits and is assigned based on the type of service and the location of the provider. Upon enrollment, Medicare Administrating Contracting (MAC) providers should receive their assigned PTAN number in their approval letter.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full [role=tabpanel]_details_&amp;:!p-3 py-4 first:border-t-0 [role=tabpanel]_&amp;:!border-none [role=tabpanel]_&amp;:!p-0 [role=tabpanel]_details_&amp;:!border-t style="word-break:break-word;overflow-wrap:break-word;hyphens:auto;-webkit-hyphens:auto;-ms-hyphens:auto"><span class="font-[550] text-primary">requestedEffectiveDate</span><span class="transition-all xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300 break-all whitespace-normal inline-flex items-center gap-1"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span><span class="px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md font-[500] text-[13px] bg-transparent ring-1 ring-inset ring-neutral-300 dark:ring-neutral-700 text-neutral-700 dark:text-neutral-300 break-all">Regex pattern:<!-- --> <code class="font-mono">^\d{8}$</code></span><span class="px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md font-[500] text-[13px] bg-transparent ring-1 ring-inset ring-neutral-300 dark:ring-neutral-700 text-neutral-700 dark:text-neutral-300 break-all">Length:<!-- --> <!-- -->8</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The requested effective date for the enrollment in YYYYMMDD format. This is the date you&#x27;d like the enrollment to take effect with the payer. For example, setting this to <code>20260601</code> for an 835 Electronic Remittance Advice (ERAs) enrollment means you want to start receiving ERAs through Stedi on that date.</p>
<p>Stedi can&#x27;t guarantee that the enrollment will be effective on this exact date. Not all payers support future dates. If the payer supports a requested effective date, Stedi will process enrollments accordingly.</p>
<ul>
<li>You can submit today&#x27;s date or a future date up to 2 years from today.</li>
<li>If not set, Stedi defaults to the submission date for the enrollment.</li>
<li>This property remains empty for <code>DRAFT</code> enrollments if not explicitly set.</li>
</ul></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full [role=tabpanel]_details_&amp;:!p-3 py-4 first:border-t-0 [role=tabpanel]_&amp;:!border-none text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The status of the enrollment. You can submit enrollments with either <code>DRAFT</code> or <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> status. The default status is <code>DRAFT</code> if not specified. When you&#x27;re ready for Stedi to begin processing the enrollment, set the status to <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>. Once an enrollment is <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>, only Stedi can set or update its status.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>DRAFT</code> - You&#x27;re still editing the enrollment and haven&#x27;t submitted it to Stedi.</li>
<li><code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.</li>
<li><code>SUBMITTED</code> - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses. If you set an enrollment request to <code>SUBMITTED</code>, Stedi treats it as <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>.</li>

14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span></span></a><div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-1 mt-3"><span class="px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md font-[500] text-[13px] bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-950/50 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300 break-all whitespace-normal inline-flex items-center gap-1"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The status of the enrollment. You can submit enrollments with either <code>DRAFT</code> or <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> status. The default status is <code>DRAFT</code> if not specified. When you&#x27;re ready for Stedi to begin processing the enrollment, set the status to <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>. Once an enrollment is <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>, only Stedi can set or update its status.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>DRAFT</code> - You&#x27;re still editing the enrollment and haven&#x27;t submitted it to Stedi.</li>
<li><code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.</li>
<li><code>PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - The enrollment requires action from the healthcare provider to proceed, such as providing additional documentation. Stedi will add a note to your enrollment request with clear instructions.</li>
<li><code>SUBMITTED</code> - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses. If you set an enrollment request to <code>SUBMITTED</code>, Stedi treats it as <code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code>.</li>
<li><code>PROVISIONING</code> - Stedi has begun the process of completing the enrollment with the payer.</li>
<li><code>LIVE</code> - The enrollment process is complete, and the specified provider can begin exchanging the listed transaction types with the payer.</li>
<li><code>REJECTED</code> - The payer rejected the enrollment. Common reasons for rejection include incorrect details in the request and that the provider is not credentialed with the payer. Customer support will contact you with reasons for rejection and next steps.</li>
<li><code>CANCELED</code> - The enrollment has been terminated per customer or provider request.</li>
</ul><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div aria-level="1" leading-[24px]"><p>This property is required for payers that require a Provider Transaction Access Number (PTAN).</p>
<p>The PTAN is a Medicare-issued number given to providers upon enrollment with Medicare. This number is usually six digits and is assigned based on the type of service and the location of the provider. Upon enrollment, Medicare Administrating Contracting (MAC) providers should receive their assigned PTAN number in their approval letter.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property -->8</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The requested effective date for the enrollment in YYYYMMDD format. This is the date the enrollment is requested to take effect with the payer. If not provided during submission, Stedi uses the submission date.</p>
<p>Stedi can&#x27;t guarantee that the enrollment will be effective with the payer on this exact date. Not all payers support future dates. If the payer supports a requested effective date, Stedi will process enrollments accordingly.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full status of the enrollment. You can submit enrollments with either `DRAFT` or `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED` status. The default status is `DRAFT` if not specified. When you're ready for Stedi to begin processing the enrollment, set the status to `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED`. Once an enrollment is `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED`, only Stedi can set or update its status.\n  - `DRAFT` - You're still editing the enrollment and haven't submitted it to Stedi.\n  - `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED` - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.\n  - `PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED` - The enrollment requires action from the healthcare provider to proceed, such as providing additional documentation. Stedi will add a note to your enrollment request with clear instructions.\n  - `SUBMITTED` - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses. If you set an enrollment request to `SUBMITTED`, Stedi treats it as `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED`.\n  - `PROVISIONING` - Stedi has begun the process of completing the enrollment with the payer.\n  - `LIVE` - The enrollment process is complete, and the specified provider can begin exchanging the listed transaction types with the payer.\n  - `REJECTED` - The payer rejected the enrollment. Common reasons for rejection include incorrect details in the request and that the provider is not credentialed with the payer. Customer support will contact you with reasons for rejection and next steps.\n  - `CANCELED` - The enrollment has been terminated per customer or provider request."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"d0:[\"$\",\"$1\",\"status\",{\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L4f\",null,{\"constraints\":{\"default\":\"$undefined\",\"pattern\":\"$undefined\",\"format\":\"$undefined\",\"multipleOf\":\"$undefined\",\"minimum\":\"$undefined\",\"exclusiveMinimum\":\"$undefined\",\"maximum\":\"$undefined\",\"exclusiveMaximum\":\"$undefined\",\"minLength\":\"$undefined\",\"maxLength\":\"$undefined\",\"minProperties\":\"$undefined\",\"maxProperties\":\"$undefined\",\"minItems\":\"$undefined\",\"maxItems\":\"$undefined\"},\"deprecated\":\"$undefined\",\"name\":\"status\",\"namespace\":\"response\",\"schema\":{\"description\":\"$101\",\"type\":\"string\",\"enum\":\"$67:props:children:props:schema:enum\"},\"type\":\"string\",\"required\":false,\"nested\":false,\"children\":[\"$L102\",[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L86\",null,{\"items\":[{\"const\":\"DRAFT\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"SUBMITTED\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"PROVISIONING\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"LIVE\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"REJECTED\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"CANCELED\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"},{\"const\":\"PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED\",\"description\":\"$undefined\"}],\"maxItems\":5}]}]]}]}]\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"d1:[\"$\",\"$1\",\"tasks\",{\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L4f\",null,{\"constraints\":{\"default\":\"$undefined\",\"pattern\":\"$undefined\",\"format\":\"$undefined\",\"multipleOf\":\"$undefined\",\"minimum\":\"$undefined\",\"exclusiveMinimum\":\"$undefined\",\"maximum\":\"$undefined\",\"exclusiveMaximum\":\"$undefined\",\"minLength\":\"$undefined\",\"maxLength\":\"$undefined\",\"minProperties\":\"$undefined\",\"maxProperties\":\"$undefined\",\"minItems\":\"$undefined\",\"maxItems\":\"$undefined\"},\"deprecated\":\"$undefined\",\"name\":\"tasks\",\"namespace\":\"response\",\"
